 23/6 brZaneba, rom-


lis Tanaxmadac tvirTebis mozidvis, drouli gatarebis da momsaxure-


bis donis amaRlebis, qveynebs Soris finansuri urTierTobis dareg-


ulirebis mizniT, `saqrkinigzaeqspedicia~ gamocxadda saqarTvelos


sarkinigzo transportis departamentis generalur eqspeditorad.


xelSekrulebis pirobaTa Tanaxmad, rkinigza uzrunvelyofda eqs-


peditoris (`saqrkinigzaeqspedicia~) gancxadebebis safuZvelze saeqs-


porto-saimporto, satranzito tvirTebis gadazidvebs romelTa


anazRaureba unda momxdariyo saqarTvelos rkinigzaze 1998-1999


wlebSi safraxto-satarifo politikiT dadgenili wesiT.


mosarCelis ganmartebiT, 1998 wlis safraxto-satarifo politikis


mixedviT, saqarTvelos rkinigzaze erTi tvirTmflobelis (eqspedi-


toris) mier safraxto wels 500 aTas tonaze meti tvirTis gadazid-


visas yovel gadametebul tonaze dawesebul iqna fasdakleba moqmed


tarifTan SedarebiT 10 procentis, xolo 1999 wels sadgur gardab-


nidan sadgur baTumamde navTobproduqtebis 500 aTas tonaze metis


925


gadazidvisas yovel gadametebul tonaze 7 aSS dolaris odenobiT,


nacvlad 8.37 aSS dolarisa.


`saqrkinigzaeqspediciam~ miuTiTa, rom man saqarTvelos rkinigzis


meSveobiT, masTan gaformebuli xelSekrulebis Tanaxmad, 1998 wels


organizeba gauwia 1 426 409.9 tona tvirTis, xolo 1999 wels 2553120


tona navTobproduqtebis gadazidvas. misi ganmartebiT, 1998-1999


wlebSi safraxto politikiT dadgenili SeRavaTis gauvrceleblobis


gamo gadamzidvelisaTvis zedmetad aris gadaxdili Sesabamisad 600 000


da 2 812 774,4 aSS dolari da moiTxova misi dabruneba.


Sps `saqarTvelos rkinigzam~ sarCeli ar cno im motiviT, rom


safraxto politikiT dadgenili SeRavaTi, misi mosazrebiT, vrcelde-


ba mxolod tvirTmflobelze, romelic aris tvirTis gamgzavni da


mimRebi, rac miTiTebulia sarkinigzo zeddebulebsa da uwyisebSi.


`saqrkinigzaeqspedicia~ ki aRniSnul dokumentebSi tvirTmflobelad


naCvenebi ar aris.


saqarTvelos rkinigzam miuTiTa samoqalaqo kodeqsis 730-e muxlis


pirvel nawilze, romelic iZleva eqspediciis xelSekrulebis cnebas da


romlis mixedviTac `eqspediciis xelSekrulebiT eqspeditori kisru-


lobs Tavisi saxeliTa da SemkveTis xarjze ganaxorcielos tvirTis


gadazidvasTan dakavSirebuli moqmedebani. SemkveTi movalea gadaixa-


dos SeTanxmebuli provizia~.


aRniSnulidan gamomdinare, rkinigzis mosazrebiT, eqspeditori


ixdis ara Tavis fuls, aramed SemkveTisas da gadazidvaze dawesebuli


tarifis gadideba an Semcireba gavlenas iqoniebs mxolod


tvirTmflobelze, xolo `saqrkinigzaeqspedicia~ tvirTmflobeli ar


aris, vinaidan is Tavisi saxeliT ar agzavnis tvirTs. amasTan, sarCelze


wardgenil SesagebelSi `saqarTvelos rkinigzam~ dadgenilad miiCnia,


rom `saqrkinigzaeqspedicia~ axorcielebda saeqspeditoro saqmi-


anobas, tvirTmflobelis tranzituli tvirTis saqarTvelos terito-


riaze gadazidvis organizacias, e.i. asrulebda saqarTvelos samo-


qalaqo kodeqsis 730-e muxliT gaTvaliswinebul movaleobas~.


Sps `saqarTvelos rkinigzam~ Segebebuli sarCeli warudgina Sps


`saqrkinigzaeqspedicias~ da moiTxova 1998 wlidan 1999 wlis 1


ivlisamde periodSi saxelSekrulebo valdebulebaTa darRveviT


vagonebis mocdenebis gamo da miyenebuli zaralis saxiT samoqalaqo


kodeqsis 394-e muxlis safuZvelze 6,924,370 laris gadaxdevineba.


SemdgomSi rkinigzam gaadida moTxovna 8.781.221 laramde.


moTxovna gaadida `saqrkinigzaeqspediciamac~. misi ganmartebiT,


2000 wlis 14 ianvris

arcerTi tvirTi ar gadauzidia. safraxto politikiT ki SeRavaTi


vrceldeboda mxolod tvirTmflobelebze, anu im pirebze, romlebic


Tavisi saxeliT axorcielebdnen tvirTis gadazidvas;

unda gamoyenebuliyo rkinigzis wesdeba, romlis 172-e muxlis mixedviT


dadgenilia, rom pretenziis an sarCelis wardgenis ufleba aqvs


tvirTis gamgzavns an mimRebs, an sxva pirs, maTi davalebiT;

miuciaT;

169-e, 177-e muxlebiT, romelic iTvaliswinebs pretenziis savaldebu-


lo wardgenas 6 Tvian vadaSi da 2 Tvian sasarCelo xandazmulobis


vadas; rkinigzis wesdebis 177-e muxliT dadgenili sasarCelo xandaz-


mulobis vada `saqrkinigzaeqspedicias~ gaSvebuli aqvs;

punqtebi). 1998 wlis safraxto-satarifo politikis mixedviT,


saqarTvelos rkinigzaze erTi tvirTmflobelis (eqspeditoris) mier


500 000  tonaze meti tvirTis gadazidvisas, yovel gadametebul tonaze

tonaze metis gadazidvisaTvis dadginda SeRavaTi yovel gadametebul


tonaze, nacvlad 8,37-isa 7 aSS dolaris odenobiT.

`saqrkinigzaeqspedicia~, safuZvels moklebulia. is warmoadgens


satransporto eqspediciis subieqts. satransporto eqspediciis

da SemkveTis xarjze ganaxorcielos ara tvirTis gadazidva, rogorc

Tu ra igulisxmeba aseT moqmedebebSi, pasuxs iZleva mxareTa Soris


dadebuli xelSekrulebebi (eqspeditoris mier aRebuli valdebulebe-


bi): aseTia, rkinigzisaTvis (gadamzidvelisaTvis) tvirTis moculobis


Sesabamisad ganacxadis miwodeba, tvirTis Tanmxlebi dokumentaciis

sxva), momsaxurebis safasuris gadaxda, gadazidvebis bazris Seswavla,


tvirTis Tanmxlebi dokumentaciis momzadeba da sxva.

dafuZnebiT. sakasacio sasamarTlo Tvlis, rom am SemTxvevaSi unda


gamoviyenoT `mewarmeTa Sesaxeb~ kanonis sawarmoTa Serwymis da gay-


ofis momwesrigebeli normebi.

48 brZanebulebis


42-e muxlis I nawilis Tanaxmad, saxelmwifo sawarmos, dawesebulebis,


organizaciis likvidaciis, reorganizaciis (Serwyma, SeerTeba, gayofa,


gamoyofa, gardaqmna) an privatizaciis SemTxvevaSi, gancxadeba


Seitaneba mis uflebamonacvle an misi qonebis bazaze dafuZnebul an


Seqmnil organizaciaSi, romelic valdebulia aanazRauros ziani.


mocemul saqmeze dadgenilia, rom samoqalaqo aviaciis qonebis


bazaze dafuZnda ramdenime sawarmo, romlebsac ar surT iyvnen ufle-


bamonacvleebi aRniSnuli valdebulebis nawilSi. `mewarmeTa Sesaxeb~


kanonis 14.6 muxlis II nawilis Tanaxmad, gayofis Sedegad warmoqmnili


sawarmoebi solidarulad ageben pasuxs Tavdapirveli sawarmos gay-


ofamde arsebul valdebulebebze.


aRniSnuli normis safuZvelze sakasacio sasamarTlos miaCnia, rom


samoqalaqo aviaciis sammarTvelos, xolo Semdgom sahaero trans-


portis departamentis qonebis bazaze dafuZnebuli da Seqmnili yvela


sawarmo aris solidaruli movale g. g-Zis mimarT.


axladSeqmnili sawarmoebidan mocemul saqmeze mopasuxed Cabmulia


mxolod sami sawarmo: Sps `saqaeronavigacia~, Sps `saqarTvelos aviax-


azebi~ da ss `Tbilisis aeroporti~, romlebic miCneul unda iqnen sol-


idarul movaleebad.


solidaruli valdebulebis mizania kreditoris mdgomareobis


gaumjobeseba. samoqalaqo kodeqsis 465-e muxlis Tanaxmad, kreditori


movalis arCevanSi Tavisufalia. mas SeuZlia moTxovna wauyenos,


rogorc yvela movales erToblivad, ise nebismier maTgans cal-calke.


samoqalaqo kodeqsis 469-e muxlis Tanaxmad, sarCelis Setana erT-erTi


solidaruli movalis mimarT kreditors ar arTmevs uflebas Seitanos


sarCeli danarCen movaleTa mimarTac.


roca erT-erTi solidaruli movale mTlianad akmayofilebs kred-


itors, solidaruli valdebuleba wydeba. xdeba valis gamstumrebeli


solidaruli movalis transformacia kreditorad danarCen soli-


darul movaleebTan mimarTebaSi. magram, Tu aRniSnuli solidaruli


movale kreditoris pretenzias ar daakmayofilebs, am ukanasknelis


mier sasamarTloSi sarCelis Setana ar arTmevs uflebas, sarCeli


Seitanos danarCen movaleTa mimarTac.


aRniSnulidan gamomdinare, g. g-Zes SeuZlia nebismier mopasuxes


erToblivad an cal-calke mosTxovos valdebulebis Sesruleba. Tu


aRniSnuli mopasuxeebi ar daakmayofileben mis moTxovnas, mas SeuZlia


sarCeli Seitanos sasamarTloSi samoqalaqo aviaciis sammarTvelos


bazaze Seqmnil danarCen sawarmoTa mimarTac. Tavis mxriv movales,


romelic solidarul valdebulebas Seasrulebs, aqvs ukumoTxovnis


ufleba danarCeni movaleebis mimarT.

saqarTvelos samoqalaqo samarTlis kodeqsis (1964 wlis


redaqciiT) 84-e muxlis Tanaxmad, sasamarTlo xandazmulobis vadis


gasvla sarCelis wardgenamde aris sarCelze uaris Tqmis safuZveli.


saapelacio palatis gadawyvetilebis gauqmebis safuZvels ar war-


moadgens is garemoeba, rom Cuqebis xelSekrulebaze xelmoweris


gamosakvlevad ar daniSnula grafikuli eqspertiza da samkurnalo


dawesebulebidan ar yofila gamoTxovili memnon kandelakis avadmy-


ofobis istoria. miTiTebuli mtkicebulebebi ver moaxdendnen raime


gavlenas sasarCelo xandazmulobis vadis gasvlaze.
